if (!is_file('doc/config_values.md')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.md');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.md')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.md');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.md') != '4dbd88be9d70f5256b3a429ced4949ef5bc5dae6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.md');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.md', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.md');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.md') !== '4dbd88be9d70f5256b3a429ced4949ef5bc5dae6') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.md') !== '561d66b66f12364f981415b776f822ad441e4b92') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.md');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.md');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.md')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.md', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.md') !== '4dbd88be9d70f5256b3a429ced4949ef5bc5dae6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.md');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'f0792f70df7e126d5f52ef9e17fa4205d0bc03b7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'f0792f70df7e126d5f52ef9e17fa4205d0bc03b7') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'c6c045bf3a27522cef3fa52507f61902a5c068f0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'f0792f70df7e126d5f52ef9e17fa4205d0bc03b7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
